msg:I took my parents to Zhangjiajie for the first time by car. I always trusted Ctrip‚Äôs quality and service, so I chose this hotel based on Ctrip‚Äôs rating list before departure. In general, the hotel's hardware is okay, there is a swimming pool, and there are many options for those who love to play in the water. However, we did not have time to experience it this time, we only wanted to stay, so we have requirements for the accommodation environment. Because it is an old hotel, after reading other people‚Äôs accommodation reviews, I was prepared not to have too high expectations for hotel facilities. I just wanted a comfortable and clean stay, so I booked their deluxe double room and parent-child room for cost-effectiveness. One night each. As a result, as shown in the picture, the reception lobby is very elegant and the room is also large. It is okay according to the picture. But the details are not good. The drinking water and bathing and toiletries are of poor quality, and the equipment is very average. It cannot be regarded as hotel level, but can only be regarded as a hotel. The bathroom was clean on the surface, but when I took a shower, I found that the water from the sewer was not good. Maybe it was because it was old. The deluxe room I booked for my parents had a musty smell as soon as I entered the door. It would be better if I opened the window for a while to ventilate it. However, I have one thing to say: when I called customer service and wanted to change a room, the customer service was still actively cooperative. This must be affirmed.
       What makes me most dissatisfied are two points:
        One is breakfast. The quality is so inconsistent! To be called a "hotel", you have to ensure that it has a certain standard, otherwise it will be called a hotel! All the food was poorly cooked, not only did it not look good, it was also unpalatable. Except for the porridge, which was better, nothing else could be called high quality.
        The second is parking management. It is particularly difficult to accept the hotel's handling of the situation. Specifically: after sleeping one night, we checked out early because we had to go to Tianmen Mountain early the next day. We also deliberately called the hotel service to ask about parking, and they were told that it could be parked there. At night, we were not informed of the charges, so we understood that residents could park for free. So, we put our luggage in our car and went out for some fun. We came back to pick up the car at around 4pm, and were told by the manager at the lobby that day: Guests who have checked out do not enjoy free parking, and emphasized that it was the hotel's policy. I couldn't change it myself, so I took the initiative to give me a discount, saying I would get a discount of 10 yuan, but only charged me 20 yuan! Oh my God! This is the first time I encountered such hotel service! I heard that it used to cater exclusively to Korean tourists. Can a hotel like this one be able to accommodate foreign tourists? I didn't plan to give such detailed feedback, so I had to take all the morning photos. It was the parking fee issue that made me particularly dissatisfied, so I'd like to express it hereü§Æ!
